In the strategy of the Stanford-Witten's work, the disk and trumpet partition functions of the fermionic/(non-)orientable JT gravity are studied on basis of the dual SYK-like models.
Furthermore, the fermionic/non-orientable JT gravity partition function has a description by a random matrix integral, and 
a correspondence between the classifications of the fermionic/(non-)orientable JT gravity
and the Dyson $\beta$-ensembles \cite{Dyson:1962es} 
and the Altland-Zirnbauer $(\alpha,\beta)$-ensembles \cite{Altland:1997zz}
is established as Table 1--4 of \cite{Stanford:2019vob}. 

The disk and trumpet partition functions for the JT supergravity are\footnote{For the disk and trumpet partition functions $Z^{\mathrm{D}}_{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta),Z^{\mathrm{T}}_{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta,L)$ computed in \cite[Appendix C]{Stanford:2019vob} from the boundary super Schwarzian path integrals,
we multiplied a factor $1/2$ is multiplied to employ the matrix model normalization \cite{Okuyama:2020qpm}:
\begin{align}
\nonumber
Z_{0,1}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta)=\frac{1}{2}Z^{\mathrm{D}}_{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta),
\quad
Z_{\mathrm{trumpet}}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta,L)=\frac{1}{2}Z^{\mathrm{T}}_{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta,L).
\end{align}
}
\begin{align}
&\label{eq:disk_SJT}
Z_{0,1}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta)
=\sqrt{\frac{1}{2\pi\beta}}\, \mathrm{e}^{\frac{\pi^2}{\beta}},
\\
&\label{eq:trumpet_SJT}
Z_{\mathrm{trumpet}}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta,L)
=\frac{1}{2\sqrt{2\pi\beta}}\, \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{L^2}{4\beta}},
\end{align}
where the parameters $\gamma$ and $\mathrm{e}^{S_0}$ of the super Schwarzian path integrals in \cite[Appendix C]{Stanford:2019vob}  are fixed to be $1/2$ 
and $1$, respectively. 
From the disk partition function $Z_{0,1}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta)$, as was done in the JT gravity, we obtain the coordinate functions 
$\sfx(z)$ and $\sfy^{\mathrm{SWP}}(z)$ in eq.\eqref{sp_curve_sw} of 
the super Weil-Petersson spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SWP}}$, 
where we employed a normalization given in \cite{Norbury:2020vyi}.
Gluing two trumpet partition functions along the geodesic circle of length $L$, we obtain the double trumpet function:
\begin{align}
\label{eq:double_trumpet_SJT}
Z_{0,2}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta_1,\beta_2)
=2\int_{\IR_+} Z_{\mathrm{trumpet}}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta_1,L)\, 
Z_{\mathrm{trumpet}}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta_2,L)\, LdL
=\frac{\sqrt{\beta_1\beta_2}}{2\pi(\beta_1+\beta_2)},
\end{align}
where we assume the JT supergravity on orientable surfaces without time-reversal symmetry,
and the factor $2$ in front of the middle integral arises from the sum over the spin structures.
The JT supergravity partition function on orientable surface with genus $g$ and $n$ wiggly boundaries without time-reversal symmetry is
\begin{align}
\label{eq:partition_function_SJT}
Z^{\mathrm{SJT}}_{g,n}(\beta_1,\ldots,\beta_n)
=
\int_{\IR_+^n}
\left(\prod_{i=1}^n2\,Z_{\mathrm{trumpet}}^{\mathrm{SJT}}(\beta_i,L_i)\right)
V_{g,n}^{\mathrm{SW}}(L_1,\ldots,L_n)\,
\prod_{i=1}^n L_idL_i,
\end{align}
where $V_{g,n}^{\mathrm{SW}}(L_1,\ldots,L_n)$ denotes the Weil-Petersson volume for the moduli space of super Riemann surfaces
computed from the supersymmetric generalization of the Mirzakhani's recursion in \cite[Appendix D]{Stanford:2019vob}.


From this double trumpet partition function, we also obtain the bidifferential $B(z_1,z_2)$ of the super Weil-Petersson spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SWP}}$ in the same way as the JT gravity,
and the super Weil-Petersson spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SWP}}=({\IP}^1;\sfx,\sfy^{\mathrm{SWP}},B)$ are obtained.
Then, the correlation functions $W^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{g,n}(z_1,\ldots,z_n)$ are 
obtained from the CEO topological recursion, and 
their inverse Laplace transforms give 
the volume polynomials $V_{g,n}^{\mathrm{SWP}}(L_1,\ldots,L_n)$ of the moduli space of super Riemann surfaces which are the supersymmetric analogue of the Weil-Petersson volumes $V_{g,n}^{\mathrm{WP}}(L_1,\ldots,L_n)$ 
and obey the ABO topological recursion. 
The Weil-Petersson volume for the moduli space of super Riemann surfaces in the JT supergravity partition function \eqref{eq:partition_function_SJT} and the super Weil-Petersson volume defined in eq.\eqref{sw_volume} are related by \cite[Section 5.3]{Norbury:2020vyi}:
\begin{align}
\label{eq:Norbury_normalization}
V_{g,n}^{\mathrm{SW}}(L_1,\ldots,L_n)
=(-1)^{n}2^{1-g}\,V_{g,n}^{\mathrm{SWP}}(L_1,\ldots,L_n).
\end{align}



\subsection{Type 0A minimal superstring}\label{sec:type0A}

It is conjectured in \cite{Okuyama:2020qpm} that the Bessel generating function $Z^{\mathrm{B}}(\hbar; \textbf{t})$ in eq.\eqref{be_pf} is obtained from the string equation \cite{Morris:1990bw,Dalley:1991qg,Dalley:1992br} for the complex matrix model which gives a non-perturbative definition of the free energy of type 0A minimal superstring \cite{Klebanov:2003wg}.%
\footnote{
The proof of the correspondence between the (generalized) BGW free energy and Kontsevich-Witten free energy
is given in \cite{YZ21,YZ23}.} 
In particular, when a finite number of variables $t_a$ is turned on such that
$t_a\ne 0$ ($1\le a\le (p-1)/2$),
the string equation gives the free energy of type 0A $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring.%
\footnote{
For the JT supergravity, the free energy is found from the string equation by tuning an infinite number of $t_a$'s.
The role of the string equation in the JT supergravity is discussed in \cite{Johnson:2019eik,Johnson:2020heh,Johnson:2020exp}.
} 

Heuristically we consider a spectral curve 
which interpolates the super Weil-Petersson spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SWP}}$ and the Bessel spectral curve
$\cC^{\mathrm{B}}$ with the coordinate functions 
in eq.\eqref{sp_curve_be}.
We obtain the $z\sfy^{\mathrm{SWP}}(z)$ and $z\sfy^{\mathrm{B}}(z)$ by differentiating $\sfy^{\mathrm{WP}}(z)$ and $\sfy^{\mathrm{A}}(z)$
of the spectral curves for the Weil-Petersson volumes and Kontsevich-Witten symplectic volumes in the bosonic models:%
\footnote{
This property will be originated from the fact that the supersymmetric formulae for the Mirzakhani-McShane identity found in \cite{Stanford:2019vob}
allows the superfield representation with fermionic coordinates.
}
\begin{align}
\label{eq:diff_super_y_1}
\sfy^{\mathrm{SWP}}(z)=\frac{1}{z}\frac{d\sfy^{\mathrm{WP}}(z)}{dz},
\qquad \sfy^{\mathrm{B}}(z)=\frac{1}{z}\frac{d\sfy^{\mathrm{A}}(z)}{dz}.
\end{align}
Adopting this heuristic relation to the $\sfy$-coordinate in eq.\eqref{sp_curve_mg} 
of the $(2,p)$ minimal string spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{M}(p)}$, 
we find the supersymmetric analogue of the $(2,p)$ minimal string 
spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$ with 
the coordinate functions in eq.\eqref{sp_curve_mg_super}.
The cut-and-join equation obtained from the spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$
is studied in Section \ref{subsec:vir_mg_super},
and we find that the generating function 
$Z^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(\hbar; \textbf{t})$ in eq.\eqref{super_mg_pf}
is obtained by the shift \eqref{shift_minimal_grav_super} for
the finite number of variables $t_a$ in 
the Bessel generating function $Z^{\mathrm{B}}(\hbar; \textbf{t})$:
\begin{align}
t_a
\quad \to 
\quad
t_a + \gamma_a
\quad \textrm{with} \quad
\begin{cases}
\gamma_a=-\frac{(-2\pi^2)^a}{(2a+1)!!a!}\prod_{i=1}^a\left(
1-\frac{(2i-1)^2}{p^2}
\right)\
& \textrm{for}\ 1 \le a \le \frac{p-1}{2},
\\
\gamma_a=0
& \textrm{for others}.
\label{shift_gamma}
\end{cases}
\end{align}
Accordingly we can regard
\begin{align}
\widehat{\mathcal{B}}(\beta_1) \cdots \widehat{\mathcal{B}}(\beta_n)\, 
Z^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(\hbar; \textbf{t})\Big|_{t_a=0}
=
\widehat{\mathcal{B}}(\beta_1) \cdots \widehat{\mathcal{B}}(\beta_n)\, 
Z^{\mathrm{B}}(\hbar; \textbf{t})
\Big|_{t_a=\gamma_a},
\label{eq:shift_p}
\end{align}
with an operator
\begin{align}
\widehat{\mathcal{B}}(\beta)=\sum_{a \ge 0} \beta^a\, \frac{\partial}{\partial t_a},
\label{boundary_op}
\end{align}
as a correlation function of type 0A $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring,
where the operator $\widehat{\mathcal{B}}(\beta)$ is considered as a boundary creation operator \cite{Okuyama:2019xbv,Okuyama:2020ncd,Okuyama:2020qpm} with a variable $\beta$ associated to a boundary.
Although we do not know the appropriate boundary condition for the disk partition function of type 0A $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring
which leads to the $\sfy$-coordinate function $\sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(z)$ in
\eqref{sp_curve_mg_super} of the spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$,
from these physical observations, we expect that
the spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$ 
is obtained from the brane partition functions in type 0A $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring.%
\footnote{
The boundary condition of the branes in type 0A minimal superstring
should be clarified from the matrix models and super Liouville field theories (e.g. \cite{Seiberg:2003nm}).}



%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\section{Derivation of the ABO topological recursion data}\label{sec:Derivation_Mirz}

Originally, the derivation of the CEO topological recursion for $\cC^{\mathrm{WP}}$ is given explicitly in \cite{Eynard:2007fi} by 
Eynard and Orantin 
from the Mirzakhani's topological recursion for the Weil-Petersson volume.
We apply their computation to the $(2,p)$ minimal string and the $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring in a reverse way (i.e. inverse Laplace transform of the CEO topological recursion), and derive the ABO topological recursion data given by
the kernel functions $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$ in eq.\eqref{eq:H_minimal}
and $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$ in eq.\eqref{eq:H_super_minimal} explicitly.

We focus on the spectral curves $\cC^{\mathrm{M}(p)}$ and $\cC^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$, 
and start from the partially (inverse) Laplace transformed CEO topological recursion for $2g-2+n > 1$:
\begin{align}
\begin{split}
\label{eq:partial_CEO}
2\, \widetilde{W}_{g,n}(z,L_K)&=
\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}\Biggl[\frac{dw}{\sfy(w)}\frac{1}{z^2-w^2}
\Biggl(
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(w,w,L_K)
\\
&\qquad\qquad\qquad\qquad\quad
+
\sum_{m=2}^n 2\, \widetilde{W}_{0,2}(w,L_m)\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\Biggr)\Biggr],
\end{split}
\end{align}
where $K=\{2,\ldots,n\}$.
In this recursion, $\widetilde{W}_{g,n}$ are partially inverse Laplace transformed correlation functions for $(g,n) \ne (0,2)$,
\begin{align}
\label{eq:tilde_W}
\int_{\IR_+^{n-1}} \widetilde{W}_{g,n}(z,L_K)\,
\mathrm{e}^{-\sum_{i=2}^n z_iL_i}\, 
\prod_{i=2}^n L_idL_i
=W_{g,n}(z,z_K), 
\end{align}
and for $(g,n) = (0,2)$,
\begin{align}
\label{eq:tilde_W_02}
\int_{\IR_+} \widetilde{W}_{0,2}(z,L_m)\, \e^{-z_mL_m}\, L_mdL_m
=W_{0,2}(z,z_m)=\frac{1}{(z-z_m)^2},
\end{align}
which gives
\begin{align}
\label{eq:W02}
\widetilde{W}_{0,2}(z,L_m)=\mathrm{e}^{zL_m}.
\end{align}
In terms of the fully inverse Laplace transformed function $V_{g,n}$ for the correlation function $W_{g,n}$:
\begin{align}
\label{eq:LD_W_V}
W_{g,n}(z,z_K)
=\int_{\IR_+^n} V_{g,n}(L,L_K)\, \mathrm{e}^{-zL-\sum_{i=2}^n z_iL_i}\,
LdL \prod_{i=2}^n L_idL_i,
\end{align}
the relation \eqref{eq:tilde_W} leads to
\begin{align}
\label{eq:tilde_W2}
\widetilde{W}_{g,n}(z,L_K)=
\int_{\IR_+} V_{g,n}(L,L_K)\, \mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, LdL.
\end{align}
In the recursion \eqref{eq:partial_CEO}, 
$\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}$ is the partially inverse Laplace transform of 
$P_{g,n}$:
\begin{align}
\label{eq:tilde_P2}
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(z,z,L_K)=
\int_{\IR_+^2} xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, \mathrm{e}^{-z(x+y)}\, dxdy,
\end{align}
where $P_{g,n}$ is the Laplace dual of $Q_{g,n}$ given by
\begin{align}
\begin{split}
\label{eq:LD_Q_P}
Q_{g,n}(z,z,z_K):=&\,
W_{g-1,n+1}(z,z,z_K)+\sum_{\substack{h+h'=g\\ J \sqcup J'=K}}^{\mathrm{stable}}
W_{h,1+|J|}(z,z_{J})\, W_{h',1+|J'|}(z,z_{J'})
\\
=&\,
\int_{\IR_+^{n+1}} xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, 
\mathrm{e}^{-z(x+y)-\sum_{i=2}^{n}z_iL_i}\, 
dxdy \prod_{i=2}^n L_idL_i.
\end{split}
\end{align}
In the following computations, we will rewrite eq.\eqref{eq:partial_CEO} into the recursion relation for $V_{g,n}$ to find the basic data 
of the ABO topological recursion.



\subsection{Derivation for $(2,p)$ minimal string}\label{sec:derivation_minimal}

We will rewrite the partially Laplace transformed CEO topological recursion \eqref{eq:partial_CEO} with the coordinate function $\sfy=\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}$ 
in eq.\eqref{sp_curve_mg} into the form of 
the Mirzakhani type ABO topological recursion \eqref{eq:Mirzakhani's} written in terms of the kernel function in eq.\eqref{eq:DR_H_bosonic} with 
$H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$:
\begin{align}
\begin{split}
\label{eq:Mirz_LD}
&
2\int_{\IR_+} V_{g,n}(L,L_K)\, \mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, LdL
\\
&=
\int_{\IR_+^3}
\left(\int_0^L H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x+y,t)\, dt\right)
xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, 
\mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, dLdxdy
\\
&\quad
+\sum_{m=2}^n \int_{\IR_+^2}
\left(\int_0^L
\left(H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t+L_m)+H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t-L_m)\right)dt \right)
\\
&\hspace{13em}\times
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\,
\mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, dLdx
\\
&=
\frac{1}{z} \int_{\IR_+^3}
xy H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x+y,t)\, P_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, \e^{-zt}\, dtdxdy
\\
&
\quad
+\sum_{m=2}^n \frac{1}{z}
\int_{\IR_+^2} 
\left(H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t+L_m)+H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t-L_m)\right)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, \e^{-zt}\, dtdx.
\end{split}
\end{align}


Firstly, we focus on the first term on the right hand side of eq.\eqref{eq:partial_CEO},
\begin{align}
\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}\,
\frac{dw}{2w\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}\left(\frac{1}{z-w}-\frac{1}{z+w}\right)
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(w,w,L_K).
\label{fst_term_p_ceo}
\end{align}
Based on the following properties:
\begin{itemize}
\item 
$\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(w,w,L_K)$ and $w \sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)$ are even functions of $w$;
\item 
$dw/\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)$ has poles at $w=u_j=(p/2\pi)\sin(j\pi/p)$ 
($j=0,\pm 1,\ldots,\pm (p-1)/2$) 
with the residue $(-1)^j\cos(\pi j/p)$ by eq.\eqref{eq:1/y};
\end{itemize}
eq.\eqref{fst_term_p_ceo} is rewritten as
\begin{align}
\label{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_1}
&
-\left[
\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}\underset{w=\pm u_j}{\mathrm{Res}}
+\underset{w=z}{\mathrm{Res}}
\right]
\frac{dw}{w\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}\frac{1}{z-w}\,
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(w,w,L_K)
\\
\nonumber
&=
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right)
\frac{2}{z^2-u_j^2}
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}\left(u_j,u_j,L_K\right)
\\
\nonumber 
&\quad\;
+\frac{1}{z}\Bigg(\frac{1}{z}
+\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right)
\left(\frac{1}{z-u_j}+\frac{1}{z+u_j}\right)\Bigg)
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(z,z,L_K)
\\
\nonumber 
&=
\frac{1}{z}\int_{\IR_+^2}
\Bigg(
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right) 
\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-u_j(x+y)}}{z+u_j}\,
+
\sum_{j=0}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right) 
\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-z(x+y)}}{z+u_j}\,
\\
\nonumber 
&\qquad\qquad\quad
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right)
\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-u_j(x+y)}-\mathrm{e}^{-z(x+y)}}{z-u_j}
\Bigg)
xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, dxdy
\\
\nonumber 
&=
\frac{1}{z}\int_{\IR_+^2}
\Bigg(
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right)
\left(\int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{e}^{-u_j(x+y+t)}\, \e^{-zt}\, dt
+\int_0^{x+y} \mathrm{e}^{-u_j(x+y-t)}\, \e^{-zt}\, dt\right)
\\
\nonumber 
&\qquad\qquad\quad
+\sum_{j=0}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{\pi j}{p}\right)
\left(\int_{x+y}^{\infty} \mathrm{e}^{+u_j(x+y-t)}\, \e^{-zt}\, dt\right)
\Bigg)
xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, dxdy.
\end{align}
Comparing the final expression with the first term in eq.\eqref{eq:Mirz_LD}, we find the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$ given in eq.\eqref{eq:H_minimal}.%
\footnote{The kernel function $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$ in eq.\eqref{eq:H_minimal} is symmetrized under the action $y\to -y$.
The extra terms which appear in the anti-symmetrization do not contribute to the integrals in the first term in eq.\eqref{eq:Mirz_LD}, 
because the Heaviside functions in the extra terms vanish in these integrals.}



\subsubsection*{Consistency check}

To check the consistency of the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$ 
derived above, we will focus on the second term on the right hand side of eq.\eqref{eq:partial_CEO}, and show the following relation:
\begin{align}
\begin{split}
\label{eq:Laplace_dual_minimal_zm}
&
\int_{\IR_+}
\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}
\Biggl[\frac{dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}\frac{2}{z^2-w^2}\,
\widetilde{W}_{0,2}(w,L_m)\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\Biggr]
\mathrm{e}^{-z_mL_m}\, dL_m
\\
&=
\frac{1}{z}\int_{\IR_+^3} 
\left(H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t+L_m)+H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t-L_m)\right)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
&\hspace{21em}
\times \e^{-zt-z_mL_m}\, dtdxdL_m.
\end{split}
\end{align}
Using the expression \eqref{eq:W02} of $\widetilde{W}_{0,2}(w,L_m)$,
we rewrite the left hand side of eq.\eqref{eq:Laplace_dual_minimal_zm} as
\begin{align}
\label{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_2}
&
\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}\,
\frac{dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}
\frac{2}{z^2-w^2}
\frac{1}{z_m-w}\, \widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&=\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}\,
\frac{dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}
\frac{1}{z^2-w^2}
\left(\frac{1}{z_m-w}+\frac{1}{z_m+w}\right)\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&=
\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}\,
\frac{2dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}
\frac{z_m}{(z^2-w^2)(z_m^2-w^2)}\, \widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&=
\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}\,
\frac{2dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}
\frac{1}{z (z_m^2-z^2)}
\left(\frac{z_m}{z-w}-\frac{z}{z_m-w}\right)
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&=
-\left[\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}\underset{w=\pm u_j}{\mathrm{Res}}
+\underset{w=z,z_m}{\mathrm{Res}}\right]
\frac{2dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(w)}
\frac{1}{z (z_m^2-z^2)}
\left(\frac{z_m}{z-w}-\frac{z}{z_m-w}\right)
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&=
\frac{2}{z (z_m^2-z^2)}\Bigg(
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right)
\left(\frac{z_m}{z+u_j}+\frac{z_m}{z-u_j}
-\frac{z}{z_m+u_j}-\frac{z}{z_m-u_j}\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{25em}
\times
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(u_j,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{7em}
+\sum_{-\frac{p-1}{2} \le j \le \frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right) \frac{z_m}{z-u_j}\,
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(z,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{7em}
-\sum_{-\frac{p-1}{2} \le j \le \frac{p-1}{2}}
(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right) \frac{z}{z_m-u_j}\,
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(z_m,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\Bigg)
\\
\nonumber
&=
\frac{2}{z (z_m^2-z^2)}
\int_{\IR_+}\Bigg(
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right)
\left(\frac{z_m\, \e^{-u_j x}}{z+u_j}-\frac{z\, \e^{-u_j x}}{z_m+u_j}\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{7em}
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right)
\left(\frac{z_m\, (\e^{-u_j x}-\e^{-z x})}{z-u_j}
-\frac{z\, (\e^{-u_j x}-\e^{-z_m x})}{z_m-u_j}\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{7em}
+\sum_{j=0}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right)
\left(\frac{z_m\, \e^{-z x}}{z+u_j}-\frac{z\, \e^{-z_m x}}{z_m+u_j}\right)
\Bigg)xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dx
\\
\nonumber
&=
\frac{2}{z}\int_{\IR_+}\Bigg(
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right)
\left(\int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{e}^{-u_j(x+t)}\, 
\frac{z_m\, \e^{-zt} - z\, \e^{-z_mt}}{z_m^2-z^2}\, dt\right.
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{15em}
+\left.
\int_0^x \mathrm{e}^{-u_j(x-t)}\, 
\frac{z_m\, \e^{-zt} - z\, \e^{-z_mt}}{z_m^2-z^2}\, dt \right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{3em}
+\sum_{j=0}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}(-1)^j\cos\left(\frac{j\pi}{p}\right)
\left(\int_x^{\infty} \mathrm{e}^{+u_j(x-t)}
\frac{z_m\, \e^{-zt} - z\, \e^{-z_mt}}{z_m^2-z^2}\, dt\right)
\Bigg)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dx.
\end{align}
On the other hand, the right hand side of eq.\eqref{eq:Laplace_dual_minimal_zm} is rewritten as follows \cite{Eynard:2007fi}:
\begin{align}
\label{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_2_2}
&
\frac{1}{z}\int_{\IR_+^2}
\left(\int_{L_m}^{\infty} \e^{-z(t-L_m)}\, H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t)\, dt
+\int_{-L_m}^{\infty} \e^{-z(t+L_m)}\, H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t)\, dt \right)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
&\nonumber
\hspace{31em}
\times \e^{-z_mL_m}\, dxdL_m
\\
&\nonumber
=
\frac{1}{z}\int_{\IR_+}
\Bigg(
\int_0^{\infty}
\left(\int_0^t \e^{-(z_m-z)L_m}\, dL_m
+\int_0^{\infty} \e^{-(z_m+z)L_m}\, dL_m \right)
\e^{-zt}\, H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t)\, dt
\\
&\nonumber
\hspace{6em}
+\int_{-\infty}^0
\left(\int_{-t}^{\infty} \e^{-(z_m+z)L_m}\, dL_m\right)
\e^{-zt}\, H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t)\, dt \Bigg)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dx
\\
&\nonumber
=
\frac{1}{z}\int_{\IR_+^2}
\left(
\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-zt}-\mathrm{e}^{-z_mt}}{z_m-z}
+\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-zt}+\mathrm{e}^{-z_mt}}{z_m+z}
\right)
H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t)\, xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dtdx,
\end{align}
where $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,-t)=H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,t)$ is used in the last equality. 
Applying the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$ in eq.\eqref{eq:H_minimal} to the final answer of eq.\eqref{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_2_2},
we find the final expression of eq.\eqref{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_2}.
Thus we derived the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{M}(p)}(x,y)$ in eq.\eqref{eq:H_minimal} of the Mirzakhani type ABO topological recursion 
for the $(2,p)$ minimal string.



\subsection{Derivation for $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring}\label{sec:derivation_super_minimal}

In the same way as the $(2,p)$ minimal string, we will rewrite the partially Laplace transformed  CEO topological recursion \eqref{eq:partial_CEO} with the coordinate function $\sfy=\sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$ 
in eq.\eqref{sp_curve_mg_super} into the form of the Mirzakhani type ABO topological recursion \eqref{eq:Mirzakhani's} written in terms of the kernel function in eq.\eqref{eq:DR_H_super} with $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$:
\begin{align}
\begin{split}
\label{eq:Mirz_LD2}
&
2\int_{\IR_+} V_{g,n}(L,L_K)\, \mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, LdL
\\
&=\int_{\IR_+^3}
xy H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x+y,L)\, P_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, \mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, 
dLdxdy
\\
&
\quad
+\sum_{m=2}^n \int_{\IR_+^2}
\left(H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,L+L_m)+H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,L-L_m)\right)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, \mathrm{e}^{-zL}\, dLdx.
\end{split}
\end{align}


Adopting the following properties:
\begin{itemize}
\item 
$\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(w,w,L_K)$ and $w \sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(w)$ are even functions of $w$;
\item
$dw/\sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(w)$ has poles at $w=\pm u_j'=\pm(p/2\pi)\sin((j-1/2)\pi/p)$ ($j=1,\ldots, (p-1)/2$)
with the residue $+u_j'(1/2\pi)(-1)^j\cos^2(\pi (j-1/2)/p)$ by eq.\eqref{eq:1/y_super};
\end{itemize}
the first term on the right hand side of the partially Laplace transformed CEO topological recursion \eqref{eq:partial_CEO} is rewritten as
\begin{align}
\label{eq:inverse_laplace_super_1}
&
-\left[
\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}\underset{w=\pm u'_j}{\mathrm{Res}}
+\underset{w=z}{\mathrm{Res}}
\right]
\frac{dw}{z-w}\frac{1}{w\sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(w)}\, 
\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(w,w,L_K)
\\
\nonumber
&=
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi}\cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(
\frac{1}{z-u_j'}-\frac{1}{z+u'_j}
\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{14em}\times
\left(\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(u_j',u_j',L_K)
-\widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(z,z,L_K)\right)
\\
\nonumber 
&\quad\;
+ \widetilde{Q}_{g,n}(z,z,L_K)\, \delta_{p,1}
\\
\nonumber
&=
\int_{\IR_+^2}
\Bigg(
\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi}\cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(
\frac{1}{z+u_j'}-\frac{1}{z-u'_j}
\right)
\left(\e^{-u_j'(x+y)}-\e^{-z(x+y)}\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{4em}
+ \e^{-z(x+y)}\, \delta_{p,1}
\Bigg)
xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, dxdy
\\
\nonumber
&=
\int_{\IR_+^2}
\Bigg(
\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi}\cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(
\int_0^{\infty} \e^{-u_j'(x+y+L)}\, \e^{-zL}\, dL
\right.
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{6em}
\left.
-\int_0^{x+y} \e^{-u_j'(x+y-L)}\, \e^{-zL}\, dL
-\int_{x+y}^{\infty} \e^{+u_j'(x+y-L)}\, \e^{-zL}\, dL
\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{4em}
+\delta_{p,1}\, \int_0^{\infty} \delta(L-x-y)\, \e^{-zL}\, dL \Bigg)
xyP_{g,n}(x,y,L_K)\, dxdy.
\end{align}
Comparing the final expression with the first term in eq.\eqref{eq:Mirz_LD2}, we find the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$ given in eq.\eqref{eq:H_super_minimal}.%
\footnote{The kernel function $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$ is given in eq.\eqref{eq:H_super_minimal} is anti-symmetrized under the action 
$y\to -y$.
The extra terms which appear in the anti-symmetrization do not contribute to the integrals in the first term in eq.\eqref{eq:Mirz_LD2}, 
because the Heaviside functions and delta functions in the extra terms vanish in these integrals.
}


\subsubsection*{Consistency check}

As the (bosonic) minimal string,  we will show the following relation
to check the consistency of the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$.
\begin{align}
\begin{split}
\label{eq:Laplace_dual_super_minimal_zm}
&
\int_{\IR_+}\underset{w=0}{\mathrm{Res}}
\Biggl[\frac{dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(w)}\frac{2}{z^2-w^2}\,
\widetilde{W}_{0,2}(w,L_m)\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\Biggr]
\mathrm{e}^{-z_mL_m}\, dL_m
\\
&=
\int_{\IR_+^3}
\left(H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,L+L_m)+H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,L-L_m)\right)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
&\hspace{21em}
\times \mathrm{e}^{-zL-z_mL_m}\, dLdxdL_m.
\end{split}
\end{align}
The left hand side of eq.\eqref{eq:Laplace_dual_super_minimal_zm} is rewritten 
in the similar way as eq.\eqref{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_2}:
\begin{align}
\label{eq:inverse_laplace_super_minimal_2}
&
-\left[\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}\underset{w=\pm u_j'}{\mathrm{Res}}
+\underset{w=z,z_m}{\mathrm{Res}}\right]
\frac{2dw}{\sfy^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(w)}
\frac{1}{z (z_m^2-z^2)}
\left(\frac{z_m}{z-w}-\frac{z}{z_m-w}\right)
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(w,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber 
&=
\frac{2}{z_m^2-z^2}\left(
-\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi} \cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(-\frac{z_m}{z+u_j'}+\frac{z_m}{z-u_j'}
+\frac{z_m}{z_m+u_j'}-\frac{z_m}{z_m-u_j'}\right)
\right.
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{28em}
\times
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(u_j',L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{1em}
+\Bigg(z_m\, \delta_{p,1}+\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi} \cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(\frac{z_m}{z-u_j'}-\frac{z_m}{z+u_j'}\right)\Bigg)
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(z,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{1em}
\left.
-\Bigg(z_m\, \delta_{p,1}+\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi} \cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(\frac{z_m}{z_m-u_j'}-\frac{z_m}{z_m+u_j'}\right)\Bigg)
\widetilde{W}_{g,n-1}(z_m,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})
\right)
\\
\nonumber 
&=
\frac{2z_m}{z_m^2-z^2}\int_{\IR_+}
\Bigg(
\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi} \cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(\frac{\e^{-u_j' x} - \e^{-z x}}{z+u_j'}
-\frac{\e^{-u_j' x} - \e^{-z x}}{z-u_j'}
\right.
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{4.5em}
\left.
-\frac{\e^{-u_j' x} - \e^{-z_m x}}{z_m+u_j'}
+\frac{\e^{-u_j' x} - \e^{-z_m x}}{z_m-u_j'}
\right)
+ \left(\e^{-z x}-\e^{-z_m x}\right)\delta_{p,1}
\Bigg)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dx
\\
\nonumber 
&=
2z_m \int_{\IR_+}
\Bigg(
\sum_{j=1}^{\frac{p-1}{2}}
\frac{(-1)^j}{2\pi} \cos^2\left(\frac{\pi}{p}\left(j-\frac12\right)\right)
\left(\int_0^{\infty} \e^{-u_j' (x+L)}\, 
\frac{\e^{-zL}-\e^{-z_mL}}{z_m^2 - z^2}\, dL
\right.
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{4.5em}
\left.
- \int_0^{x} \e^{-u_j' (x-L)}\, 
\frac{\e^{-zL}-\e^{-z_mL}}{z_m^2 - z^2}\, dL
- \int_x^{\infty} \e^{+u_j' (x-L)}\, 
\frac{\e^{-zL}-\e^{-z_mL}}{z_m^2 - z^2}\, dL
\right)
\\
\nonumber
&\hspace{4.5em}
+ \delta_{p,1}\, \int_{0}^{\infty} \delta(L-x)\, \frac{\e^{-z L}-\e^{-z_m L}}{z_m^2 - z^2}\, dL
\Bigg)
xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dx.
\end{align}
On the other hand, similar to eq.\eqref{eq:inverse_laplace_minimal_2_2}, 
the right hand side of eq.\eqref{eq:Laplace_dual_super_minimal_zm} is rewritten as
\begin{align}
\label{eq:inverse_laplace_super_minimal_2_2}
2z_m \int_{\IR_+^2}
\left(
\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-zt}-\mathrm{e}^{-z_mt}}{z_m-z}
+\frac{\mathrm{e}^{-zt}-\mathrm{e}^{-z_mt}}{z_m+z}
\right)
H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,L)\, xV_{g,n-1}(x,L_{K\setminus \{m\}})\, dLdx,
\end{align}
where $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,-L)=-H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,L)$ is used. 
Applying the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$ in eq.\eqref{eq:H_super_minimal} to eq.\eqref{eq:inverse_laplace_super_minimal_2_2}, the final expression of eq.\eqref{eq:inverse_laplace_super_minimal_2} is found. 
Thus, 
the consistency equation eq.\eqref{eq:Laplace_dual_super_minimal_zm} 
for the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$ is verified, and 
the CEO topological recursion for the spectral curve $\cC^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}$ is shown to be equivalent to
the Mirzakhani type ABO topological recursion with the kernel function $H^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}(x,y)$.

\section{Tables of volume polynomials}\label{sec:table_vol}

In this appendix, we give some computational results of the volume polynomials 
for the 2D gravity models and their Masur-Veech type twist.

\subsection{Volume polynomials}\label{sec:table_vol_no_twist}
\quad


\begin{longtable}[l]{ccl}
\caption{Weil-Petersson volumes}
\label{lst_wp}
\endfirsthead
%\hline
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{0,3}$ &$=$& 
$1$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{1,1}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{\pi^2}{12} + \frac{1}{48}L_1^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{0,4}$ &$=$& 
$2\pi^2 + \frac12\sum_{i=1}^4 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{1,2}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{\pi^4}{4} + \frac{\pi^2}{12}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^2
+\frac{1}{192}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^4 + \frac{1}{96} L_1^2L_2^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{0,5}$ &$=$& 
$10\pi^4 + 3\pi^2\sum_{i=1}^5 L_i^2 
+\frac{1}{8} \sum_{i=1}^5 L_i^4 + \frac12 \sum_{1\le i<j\le 5} L_i^2L_j^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{1,3}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{14\pi^6}{9} + \frac{13\pi^4}{24} \sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^2 
+ \frac{\pi^2}{24} \sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^4 
+ \frac{\pi^2}{8} \sum_{1\le i<j\le 3} L_i^2L_j^2
+ \frac{1}{1152} \sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^6$ 
\\
& &
$+ \frac{1}{192} 
\sum_{\begin{subarray}{c} 
1\le i, j\le 3\\ (i\ne j)
\end{subarray}} 
L_i^2 L_j^4
+ \frac{1}{96} L_1^2L_2^2L_3^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{WP}}_{2,1}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{29\pi^8}{192} + \frac{169\pi^6}{2880}L_1^2
+ \frac{139\pi^4}{23040}L_1^4 + \frac{29\pi^2}{138240}L_1^6
+ \frac{1}{442368}L_1^8$

\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SMV}}_{2,5}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{135\pi^2}{16}+\frac{135}{32}\sum_{i=1}^5 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SMV}}_{3,1}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{23\pi^4}{1024}+\frac{51\pi^2}{4096}L_1^2+\frac{15}{8192}L_1^4$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SMV}}_{3,2}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{115\pi^4}{1024}+
\frac{225\pi^2}{4096}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^2 + 
\frac{75}{8192}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^4 + \frac{63}{2048} L_1^2L_2^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SMV}}_{3,3}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{345\pi^4}{512}+
\frac{765\pi^2}{2048}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^2 + 
\frac{225}{4096}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^4 + \frac{189}{1024} 
\sum_{1\le i<j\le 3} L_i^2L_j^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SMV}}_{4,1}$ &$=$& 
$\frac{1827\pi^6}{32768} + \frac{473\pi^4}{16384} L_1^2+
\frac{625\pi^2}{131072} L_1^4 +\frac{175}{524288} L_1^6$
\\
%\hline
\end{longtable}



\begin{longtable}[l]{ccl}
\caption{Twisted super Weil-Petersson volumes}
\label{lst_super_wp_tw_s}
\endfirsthead
%\hline
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{0,n}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$0$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{1,n}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{(n-1)!}{8}$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{2,1}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{3(6s+1)\pi^2}{128}+\frac{3}{256}L_1^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{2,2}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{9(8s+1)\pi^2}{128}+\frac{9}{256}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{2,3}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{9(10s+1)\pi^2}{32}+\frac{9}{64}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{2,4}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{45(12s+1)\pi^2}{32}+\frac{45}{64}\sum_{i=1}^4 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{2,5}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{135(14s+1)\pi^2}{16}+\frac{135}{32}\sum_{i=1}^5 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{3,1}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{(1362 s^{2}+255 s+23)\pi^4}{1024}
+\frac{3(168 s+17)\pi^2}{4096}L_1^2+\frac{15}{8192}L_1^4$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{3,2}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{(9684 s^{2}+1530 s+115)\pi^4}{1024}+
\frac{3(1008s+85)\pi^2}{4096}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^2$ 
\\
& &
$+ \frac{75}{8192}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^4 + \frac{63}{2048} L_1^2L_2^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{3,3}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{3(13062 s^{2}+1785 s+115)\pi^4}{512}+
\frac{9(1176 s+85)\pi^2}{2048}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^2$
\\
& &
$\frac{225}{4096}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^4 + \frac{189}{1024} 
\sum_{1\le i<j\le 3} L_i^2L_j^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SWP}}_{4,1}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\frac{(1115332 s^{3}+216788 s^{2}+26488 s+1827)\pi^6}{32768} + 
\frac{(106911 s^{2}+14643 s+946)\pi^4}{32768} L_1^2$
\\
& &
$+ \frac{125(69 s+5)\pi^2}{131072} L_1^4 +\frac{175}{524288} L_1^6$

\end{longtable}



\begin{longtable}[l]{ccl}
\caption{Twisted volume polynomials of the $(2,2p-2)$ minimal superstring}
\label{lst_super_mst_twist_s}
\endfirsthead
%\hline

\\

$\frac{(n-1)!}{8}$

\\

$\left[540s\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)+45\right]\frac{\pi^2}{32}
+ \frac{45}{64}\sum_{i=1}^4 L_i^2$
\\

$\left[1890s\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)+135 \right]\frac{\pi^2}{16}
+ \frac{135}{32}\sum_{i=1}^5 L_i^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}_{3,1}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\left[\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)
\left(6s^2\left(227-\frac{27}{p^2}\right)+255s \right)+23 \right]
\frac{\pi^4}{1024}$
\\
& &
$+ \left[504s\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)+51\right]\frac{\pi^2}{4096}L_1^2
+ \frac{15}{8192}L_1^4$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}_{3,2}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\left[\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)
\left(36s^2\left(269-\frac{69}{p^2}\right)+1530s \right)+115 \right]
\frac{\pi^4}{1024}$
\\
& &
$+ \left[3024s\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)+255 \right]
\frac{\pi^2}{4096}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^2 
+ \frac{75}{8192}\sum_{i=1}^2 L_i^4 + \frac{63}{2048} L_1^2L_2^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}_{3,3}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\left[\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)
\left(126s^2\left(311 - \frac{111}{p^2}\right)+5355s \right)+345 \right]
\frac{\pi^4}{512}$
\\
& &
$+ \left[10584s\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)+765 \right]
\frac{\pi^2}{2048}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^2 
+ \frac{225}{4096}\sum_{i=1}^3 L_i^4$ 
\\
& &
$+ \frac{189}{1024} 
\sum_{1\le i<j\le 3} L_i^2L_j^2$
\\
$\VO^{\mathrm{SM}(p)}_{4,1}[\sfm]$ &$=$& 
$\left[\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)
\left(4s^3\left(278833 - \frac{44866}{p^2} + \frac{1233}{p^4}\right)
\right.\right.$
\\
& &
$\left.\left.\qquad
+ 4s^2\left(54197 - \frac{19197}{p^2}\right)+26488s \right)+1827 \right]
\frac{\pi^6}{32768}$
\\
& &
$+ \left[\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)
\left(3s^2\left(35637 - \frac{12637}{p^2}\right)+14643s \right)+946 \right]
\frac{\pi^4}{32768} L_1^2$
\\

$+ \left[8625s\left(1-\frac{1}{p^2}\right)+625 \right]\frac{\pi^2}{131072} L_1^4
